## Instruction

Today we have 3 new employees joining us, and each employee's information is stored in the Snowflake database.

Based on the employee's group assignment and training manual, automatically generate training task lists, send emails to the employee's email address, and update the task content and planned completion dates to the database.

For new employees, send onboarding emails in the following format:

```
Dear xxx, You have the following training tasks to complete:
xxx
xxx
xxx
Please complete them as soon as possible.
```

Additionally, you need to check for employee records where the current date has exceeded the training completion deadline but the task status is still "incomplete", send reminder emails to the employees themselves in the same format.

The order of the tasks in the email should be based on the order in the training manual.

And remember to CC their direct supervisor.

You can view the database build process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/landing-task-reminder/preprocess).

```json arguments
{
	"query":"SELECT e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 e.NAME,
	 e.EMAIL,
	 e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	 el.LANDING_DATE,
	 el.LANDING_TASK_ASSIGNED\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE_LANDING el\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON e.EMPLOYEE_ID = el.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE el.LANDING_DATE = CURRENT_DATE();"
}
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```json arguments
{
	"query":"WITH emp AS (\n  SELECT e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 e.NAME,
	 e.EMAIL,
	 e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n         CASE WHEN s.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'BACKEND'\n              WHEN f.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'FRONTEND'\n              WHEN t.EMPLOYEE_ID IS NOT NULL THEN 'TESTING' END AS GRP\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e\n  LEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND) s ON s.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.REPORT_TO_ID\n  LEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND) f ON f.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.REPORT_TO_ID\n  LEFT JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT EMPLOYEE_ID FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING) t ON t.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.REPORT_TO_ID\n  WHERE e.EMPLOYEE_ID IN (9001,
	9002,
	9003)\n),
	 sup AS (\n  SELECT EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 NAME AS SUP_NAME,
	 EMAIL AS SUP_EMAIL\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE\n  WHERE EMPLOYEE_ID IN (8001,
	8002,
	8003)\n)\nSELECT emp.*,
	 sup.SUP_NAME,
	 sup.SUP_EMAIL\nFROM emp\nJOIN sup ON sup.EMPLOYEE_ID = emp.REPORT_TO_ID;"
}

```

```json output_result
type: data
data_id: 48794052-dd69-4dd5-8b5f-297413258a20
data:
- EMPLOYEE_ID: 9003
  NAME: Maria Hernandez
  EMAIL: hernandezm@mcp.com
  REPORT_TO_ID: 8003
```

```json arguments
{
	"query":"WITH overdue AS (\n  SELECT 'BACKEND' AS GRP,
	 b.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 b.TASK_NAME\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND b\n  WHERE b.FINISHED_FLAG = FALSE AND b.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n  UNION ALL\n  SELECT 'FRONTEND' AS GRP,
	 f.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 f.TASK_NAME\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND f\n  WHERE f.FINISHED_FLAG = FALSE AND f.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n  UNION ALL\n  SELECT 'TESTING' AS GRP,
	 t.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 t.TASK_NAME\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING t\n  WHERE t.FINISHED_FLAG = FALSE AND t.DDL < CURRENT_DATE()\n),
	 emp AS (\n  SELECT e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 e.NAME,
	 e.EMAIL,
	 e.REPORT_TO_ID\n  FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e\n)\nSELECT o.GRP,
	 o.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 emp.NAME,
	 emp.EMAIL,
	 emp.REPORT_TO_ID,
	 o.TASK_NAME\nFROM overdue o\nJOIN emp ON emp.EMPLOYEE_ID = o.EMPLOYEE_ID\nORDER BY o.EMPLOYEE_ID;"
}

```
